<p>Ka pa chuan, "Vanhnuailiana pa, Taia te awmnaah chuan chuti ang chaw te chu kan siam malek ang maw le. Antam tuihang tho kan in ang chu," a lo ti fiamthu a.</p>
<p>Tirhkoh Buka nupuia pa hi tun hmaa zu hmun sa hmuna cheng thin a ni a, a fanu hmingah pawh Zulawmi an ti a. Mahse, Kristian a lo nih hnuin a hming chu a zahpui a, Lallawmi tiin a thlâk ta a. Ama fate pawh awmze mumal nei takin an sa a. An fapa upa zawk chu Kristiana an luh chawiin Lalluta an ti a, a naupang zawk chu Pathian thatna chawiin Lalthaa an ti thung a.</p>
<p>I sa chhum chu a va rimtui cham cham ve!</p>
<p>Mizo pa chuan a hna a zo tih entir nan 'Churchilla' lam chu hawiin a han thle deuh bak a, 'Churchhilla' chu mi thianghlim ṭawngṭai tur ang deuh hian a kut pahnih chu a hmui zawnah a han dah bukthuah a, "He hun i rawn hmang thei hi a lawmawm kan ti khawp mai," a han ti a. Ka ṭhiante zawng zawng chu General Knowledge tlem tal an zawt vek nia ka hriat aṭangin a tihtawpna tur ṭawngkam a nih ka la ring phak hauh lova. Eng emaw tal min la zawh ve ka rin tlat aṭangin a chhak lama thu Hnar Vahaia chu ka han en a, "Thank You" tih pahin a nui vun vun a, a thle deuh nu nu bawk a, a chhak leha thu 'Parthasarathy' lah chuan nui chungin min melh a, "Thank You" a ti ve leh mai a. "Haw tawh rawh" min tihna a ni tih ka la hre thiam ta lo cheu a. Churchilla chu ka zuk en leh a, ani lah chu a lo hawi hai vel mai mai tawh si a. Thil awmzia ka hre tan dawn chiah tih chuan Mizo pa chuan Mizo tawngin, "A! A tawk tawh e, an zo tawh a nih kha!" a ti ta roh a.</p>
<p>Rambuai phat aṭang khân fiahna pawh awm lo, rinhlelh thu-ah sipai leh police uniform ha tawh phawt chuan charge-na mumal vak pawh awm lovin an rinhlelh tawh phawt chu MNF mi leh sa dik tak angin Jail-ah Mizo tam tak an khung a. Chu bâkah chuan MNF mi leh sa kori tu tham lêm lo MNF-a inpe ve maite kum 3 kum 4 tàntir te an awm teuh bawk a. General Amnesty puan a nih chuan khatianga Jail tangte kha chhuah vek tûr an ni. Chu bâkah MNF mi leh sa, hrisêl lohna vâng emaw, eng vâng pawha underground thei tawh lote an in lam an rawn hnaih khân man an ni bawk a. General Amnesty puan a nih chuan chutiang mi zawng zawng chu chhuah zalên vek tûr an ni a. India Constitution-ah Law & Order vawn chu State list a mi a nih aṭangin General Amnesty puan hi Assam Sorkar thuneihna liau liau a ni. Chutiang bawkin MNF leh Central sorkar inbiak phalna Clearance chu Assam sorkar thu thu a ni bawk. He Amnesty min phalsak hnu hian Batch hmasa ber an han chhuah chhin phawt a, Zoram dinhmun an han thlir leh vang vang a. MNF lamah India tan nghawng tha lo an hmuh loh hnuah Batch pahnihna, chutiang zelin pathumna, palina, pangana leh a hnu zel pawh zawi zawiin an chhuah a, Prime Minister Indira Gandhi-in January ni 21, 1972-a ngaihdamna runpui Mizoram UT a rawn puan ruala a puan kha chuan MNF mi leh sa tang leh a kaihhnawiha lo tang ve ringawt te kha chhuah fel an ni ta.</p>
<p>Chu zawngin beiseina inchherchhuan min rawn chhawp teh meuh mai le.</p>
<p>Mizo lalte hian phai vai in run fo thin a. Kum 50 vel chhûng khan vawi sawmhnih chuang in dep ram Assam phai in run a. Sap naupang hial salah te in man a. Tunah hian Sipaiin beihpui meuh thlâkin kan rawn hmachhawn ta che u a ni. Kumpinu lung in tihawi loh chuan nasa takin kan kap ang che u. Kan silai thatziate hi in hre lo em ni? Kap rawh.</p>
<p>Ramhuai dawithiam pitarte kha i lo hmu em?</p>
<p>Kalkawngah pawh i nau hi i nghak zel dawn nia. An kalna lam chu in hria maw?</p>
<p>Thihna hian thih awm tawh lohna hmun hlutzia min hrilh a duh bawk. Chatuan ropuizia leh lungngaih leh nat awm tawh lohna Vânram hlutzia pholangtu a ni a, chumi châk chuan ni tin zin kawng kan zawh zâwk thin. Thihna chu kan chatuan hmun thlen theihna tûra ramri kânna a ni. Thi lo chuan tholeh tûr kan awm dâwn lo. Thihna siama chatuan nunna siamtu hian fak a va phû êm, a lo rem hre ber e.</p>
<p>Kanârkhual kan tichhuak palha, in lo hmu mial lo maw?</p>
<p>Faustus, tunah hian engang dinhmunah chiah nge i awm ? 1 khawngaihthlâk hle a, ithiltihte hi eng nge ni ngaihturah rawh. Chhandamna chang tlak pawh i ni tawh lo va, i hmabak chu lungngaihna leh thihna a ni ringawt tawh mai. Hremhmun kawngka chu i tan a inhawng a, a ko mek bawk che, i tawpna chu a hnai takzet ta. Faustus-a hian a phu tawk hremna chu a hmu dawn mek a nih hi.</p>
<p>Mahni lam inthian thianghlimin, aṭang hle tak mai a.</p>
<p>Hla phuah chhan tawi fel takin a sawi ang.</p>
<p>Phungrual chinlai ngai ing e.</p>
<p>Tunah zawng ngaih a tha ta, a let ta zuah mai.</p>
<p>A tawnna hi pawh mar deuh a ngai a nih hi.</p>
<p>Operation Armoury-a in han kal kha i la hriaṭang tiraw?</p>
<p>Nghalthianga er êm êmtu Hautuka chu a phûr zual a, "Chhei chhei raw! Khuarelin a nang dâwn e," a ti a. Mahse, Ainâwni chu mi aṭang maiin a ding reng a. Darchheuva chuan a aw a'n thian a, fir ngialin Nghalthianga chu a melh a, "Chu. kan zâl lo tiin i pha leh si em ni?" a han ti a. A awkâ chu a dengkhawng lek lek a.</p>
<p>Pari pa hi Joint Director a ni a, Mizoram sawrkar-a department pakhatah. Mahse, a pension hma kum nga la awmah cancer natna aṭangin a thi a. A pa thih hnu aṭang hian a nu chuan dam tih a nei ta lo va, a taksa chak loh vang pawh a ni ang, thawhah a vei zui ta a. Khumah chuan a awm ta chawt mai a ni.</p>
<p>Naupangin nau an paw thle ngêk ngêk fo.</p>
<p>Chutiang bawkin, Mizo officer, Mizoram pawna sawrkar hna thawkte pawhin, an awmna lam mite thawnthu leh an khawtlang nun te, an tawng kalhmangte hi Mizo tawngin ziak thin ta sela, kan hnam hian kan ṭangkaipui ngei ngei ang a, literature-ah hmasawnna kawng tha tak a ni thei nghal bawk ang. Chhuna eizawnna pangngai, sawrkar hna thawh hun bakah hian kan lehkha thiamte hian, "Ka buai em atin ni." an tihna chhan hi lehkhabu an buatsaih vang ni zawk sela chuan, hma kan sawn nasa lehzual ngei dawn a ni.</p>
<p>An zinga pakhat chuan fiamthu a thawh a, an lo nui dar dar hlawm a.</p>
<p>A ni teh tak e, a ni ber a awm lohvin khuang lova chai ang chauh a ni ang asin!</p>
<p>Hei hi Krismas hlaa tlaizawng par lan hmasak berna leh, Mizo rilrua tlaizawng par leh Krismas a lan kawp tanna a lo ni ta a ni. Thlarau mita a thil ente chu a hmu chiang hle niin a lang, Bawng in tlawmah ka Lal riangvai tak saw, A chun riang Marin a chawi e.</p>
<p>A lungawi lo khawp a, a rûm ngal ngal a!</p>
<p>Tunah hian he Coronavirus hi a thawh hnihna chu khawthlang lam lamah te leh India ram, a bik takin Maharashtra lamah te namen loin a darh leh mek a. March 2021 chhûng hian ram hrang hrang an in-lockdown leh ta chuah chuah mai. Saudi Arabia-ah chuan thlawh luh leh thlawh chhuah khap tlat a ni a, Tanzania pawhin Total Lockdown a puang leh ta. Spain pawhin Emergency March thla chhûnga pawhsei turin a puang bawk a, UK chuan thla khat Lockdown a puang leh ta a, France-in kar hnih Lockdown a puang a, Germany chuan thla khat tawp Lockdown a puang ve leh ta. Italy pawn Total Lockdown a puang leh ta. Heng ram te hian he Covid-19 thawh hnihna hi a hma aia chak zawk leh hlauhawm zawk niin an sawi.</p>
<p>Kan sawrkar department building thar neih ho pawh kuhva kan eina chinai kan tat var ngiai nguai a, kan chhak sen ngei nguai mai te hi sim vat a hun tawh a ni.</p>
<p>Ka message hmuh chu ka hre chhuak leh a. Tunah a khawsik a tlun nasa. A khumah awm daih ta se, engtin nge min chhan theih reng reng ang ni?</p>
<p>Mizo tawng grammar-ah hian verb leh adverb tang dun hi 'verb'leh 'adverb' anga an in-qualify tawn phawt chuan thu mal anga ziah zawm tur a ni ngai lo tih hi hriat tur a ni. Mizo tawng grammar-ah phei chuan verb leh adverb tang dun chu kan sentence-ah subject emaw, ob-ject emawa kan hmana, noun anga an tan dun phawt chuan 'noun phrase' emaw, 'gerund phrase'emaw a ni zel thin a; noun sawi fiahtua kan hman chuan 'participle phrase' a la ni ta thin bawk a. Chutianga 'noun phrase' leh 'gerund phrase'leh 'parti-ciple phrase atân tea kan hmannaah pawh chuan verb leh adverb tang dun chu thu mal anga ziah zawm tur a ni lo tih hi grammar lam sawi ve thin chuan kan hriat fiah a hun tawh hle.</p>
<p>Hawh u, thla hi la zel ila, nakina kan lung tileng tur te, kan hriat reng duh thilte hi dah that turin i khawl zel ang u. Mahse, mi dang thlalak, hmuhnawm lo leh rilru natna thlen theitu lak erawh sim ila, pawimawh atana lak a ngai a nih erawh chuan a thlenna tur dikah chauh thlentirin mi zawng zawng hmuh theiha tlangzarhtu nih hi i sim ang u.</p>
<p>Duh lai, ka va ngai tak che êm!</p>
<p>Kei pawhin aw, na tawkin le.</p>
<p>An mitha si a, an hmel a tha bawk si a, anmahni reng reng pawh hi hmeichhe tha tak niin an lan hi maw, a ti a. Chutia mi ta tur awma han sawi pawh chu Chalkunga chuan nuam a ti lo hle mai a. An kar chu hla hle angin lang mah sela a rilru tak chuan a inbel ve hle si a, a hmeichhiatna lo ngaizawng ve ta napui chu. Chu lo rengah pawh dan naranin tleirawl laia ngaihzawng ber te chu mahni neih tur ngeia ngaihna hi a awm si thin a. Mahni ngaihzawng tak mai te chu mi tana bel hi a har viau reng mai a ni. Chu chu a hmei a pa tan a har a ni. Tichuan, an kal zel chu bâwng rual hi an hmu a, Chalkunga chuan a um ta a. Thanghrima chuan Kawlrit rual a um bawk a, an inthen ta a, chumi ni chuan an inthen hlen ta a. An inhmu leh ta reng reng lo va.</p>
<p>Ka zin chu ka lo haw leh tawh a, Lalliana nen inhmuh a ṭul a, in la eng teh iar a, ka lo lut thla rawk a, mut te hi in lo tum reng tawh ang e?</p>
<p>Ba chhum hmin sa hi ba khovah bun rawh u.</p>
<p>Pu Duma chuan, "Ni e, a nau hmuak tûrin Ngûri chu a kal a ni lek tak ang. Kan hnathawh bàn veleh in lam chu a pan zêl kha maw," a ti a. An sawi zo chauh tih chuan naupang kum sawm leh pahnih vêl lek ni âwma lang hian tiang hawlin di in te tak tê chu a rawn zawng phei dê dê a, kawta bawngpui ding chu a rawn hnawt kiang a. Ngûri nau Chuma chu a ni. Mit khing hnih del saa piang a ni a, mahse a ding lam pang chuan a hmu deuh riai ruai a, a kal thanna leh an in vêla thilte chu harsa lo takin a hre ve thei.</p>
<p>Ka do Run ralin, hnamchem chawi lo, Thainu rual min ti, ka do Run ralin.</p>
<p>Nia, a thih chhan kha chhui dawn dan a ni vek a, a dik chiah e zawng kan ti ngam lo nain, a ui fingte khan an entir chiang hleah kan ngai. Chu bakah Pu Laihnuna'n a duhthusam a lo sep thin aṭangin an chhui dawn zel a, a in phaman tha khawp mai. Kan val upa pakhat sawi danin, Hnuna hian a duhthusam a sawi fo chu, zukchal kaphliam ila, tuiah zuang lut se, chumi hliam tuia hnim hlum chu ka chak ber, a ti thin a Khami ni khan zukchal a hliam a, a duhthusam ang ngeiin Tlawng luiah sa hliam chu a zuang lut a. Ani Hnuna leh a ui hruaite khan ûm zuiin tuiah an inbei ta chiam a, an inbei rei hle a ni ang ui chezia aṭang khan. Mahse sahliam chu a lo la chak êm a, an putu paw'n an hneh ta ngang lo a, chu a hnu hmanah a vanduaia siamin Hnuna bekah sazuk hliam chuan a beng fuh a, a che hlei thei ta lo a, tuiah a inhai buai zui a, a uifingte'n sahliam hlir an buaipui bawk nen, an pu chu puih nachâng an hre lawk si lo a. a tlin ta lo ni berin a lang.</p>
<p>Tute nge ni? Zan tlai tawha he lai hmuna la vâk la vâk?</p>
<p>Ni khat chu, Chhura hian an banglaia a nupui pawnfên thisen kai inzar hi a va hmu a. A nupuiin, "A sen reng reng chu hlau zel ang che," a tih kha a la hre reng a. Feipui leh phaw a chuh a,</p>
<p>A pa Tlutpawrha'n Halkha a rawt chiam lai khan Vandula hi ralkai chin a ni tawh a. Halkha rawt hi Mizo Chanchin tih ziaktu Rev. Liangkhaia'n Chhipphira an awm laia thil thleng niin a ziak. Chutihrualin, Mizo Chanchin tih ziaktu tho B.Lalthangliana chuan Halkha Rawt hi kum 1860 kum vela thleng niin a ring thung a. Hei erawh a dik hlel deuh maithei, Vanlalvuana Sailo leh Lalsangzuali Sailo te ziah anga Vandula hi kum 1820 chhoa piang a nih chuan Halkha Rawt hi 1860 daiha tlangval tantirh, a pa Tlutpawrha hunlaia thil thleng a thleng thei a ni lo, a chhan chu Halkha Rawt hi Vandula nih hmel.</p>
<p>Inkhawm bâna lêng kan ni bawk a, zân a lo rei dâwn ta mai a, Liani chuan lehkha te min zial sak hlawm a, thingpui min lum bawk a, hlim taka kan inkawm tlân hnu chuan kan ṭin ta a. Kei chu in danga ka ṭhiante-ho hnênah ka riak a. Zinga ka hawn chuan ka thlen in nula Hmingpuii chuan "Nizân i lênnaah theihnghilh eng nge i neih i hria em?" min lo ti a.</p>
<p>Mamawh changkang tial tial a, khawvel chanchin zau zawka kan han hriat theih hnu hian, Mizote zingah dan leh hrai ṭangkaina leh hlutna kan hre chho ve zel a. Dan hriatloh hi chhuanlam tling a nih loh laiin, mi nawlpui tan dan hriat ve ngawt hi thil harsa tak a ni a. Dan zirna in te chu awm ve bawk mah se, tam tak tan heng hmun aṭanga te a dan han zir mai chu thil theih a ni lova. Tin, mahni eizawn nana hmang lo tur tan phei chuan a hranpa a han zir ngat te hi thil harsa leh hun khawhralna mai anga a ngaih theih hial a. Chuti chung chung chuan khawthlanga kan khawsak honaṭangah te leh kan nitin nun phungah dan leh hrai pawimawhna a lo pung chho zel ta mai bawk si.</p>
<p>Chu thawnthu bu hming chu Lalramchhana tih a ni a, a ziaktu chu Ramhmangaiha a ni. Publisher a awm lo va, chhuah kum leh copy zat tih ang chi kha a awm miah lo bawk.</p>
<p>Tu dài, tu dawl ziah danah an buai:</p>
<p>Kum a lo tawp dawn a, buh an han seng zawh chuan Krismas a lo ni leh mai dawn si a. Pi Riali chuan a huphurh em em mai a. Lusun anga a han awm tak tak dawn chuan, a thi tih hriat chianna a la awm tak tak si lo va. A la dam tih dawn leh, a hmel hmuh tur awm chuang bawk si lo chu a nu rilru tihrehawmtu ber a ni a. Kum a lo vei dawn meuh zawngin a beiseina pawh a tlem ve ta tial tial a. Buh seng an zo va, an han thiar zawh vek hnu, Krismas hma ni 4 velah Kristianho chu an thukhawm a, Thangbawnga chungchang an ngaihtuah ho va. Beisei tur awm tawh lo, thi anga pawm mai tawh tur, an ti ta a. A nu chuan a la ui viau nain ui thei a ni bik tawh lo va, thlan thu an ni ta nghal mai a. Chutia an inhmuhkhawm takah chuan Krismas ro te an rel ta nghal bawk a.</p>
<p>Kan thil sawi tifiah turin thu la chhawng lawk i la:</p>
<p>Chutiang lam a ni lo. Zahnih zingah sawm chiah an la dawn a. Tling awm deuh deuh tlangval pali ka hria. Chu mite chuan min hre bawk. try mai dawn 'ni! Zahnih zinga sawm thlan chhuah nih tum ai chuan pass ngei ngei tur pali zinga pakhat nupui nih tum mai hi a awl fe zawk!</p>
<p>Vansenin ka hluikhuang lo chhang ang che,</p>
<p>Hello Sir. Vanchengpui daiah. aw, an zinga mi pakhat a thi. rin aiin a hnawk ril hmel a, rawn fimkhur ang che u. Thihthiapho alawm le. kawngah mau tlawn pahnih kan lo kham ang. sumo service pangngai tak angin aw. ka GPS rawn track tel mai rawh. tun aṭanga darkar li leh a chanveah kan lo beisei ang che u.top priority rawn pe hram rawh u aw. thanks. ok. <p>Pindan aṭangin U Mawitei a lo chhuak a. Keini thianzaho min han hmuh chuan a hmaa Muanaten tha an lo tih thu an sawi kha ka lo hrilh tawh bawk nen. A rawn nui sâng a.</p>
<p>Taxi-ah i chuanin midang nen in-share loh theih hram tum ang che. I bul ami khan covid hrik a pai em tih i hre lo a ni. Fimkhur tluk a awm lo a ni.</p>
<p>Hlaa pi leh puten an lo chawi thin pawh hi darbu a ni deuh ber a, chung zinga tlemte han tarlang ila: Kan Siallam dar, Siallam dar, Khua tinin min sel lo u, Luh sum rawn chawi sial rawn chawi, tih te.</p>
<p>Mangan naka laia nang mi â pui lah hi i lo puak ve phawng phawng a.</p>
<p>Hluni chuan, "Châka hmuam reng ah kan ti hlei nêm, in tawh mah ula kan thingpui in la in ve lo tlat a," tih pahin an hma-ah chuan a hûn a.</p>
<p>Ruai siamna hâr mei pawh a mit duak tawh a nih hi.</p>
<p>Mi sual tak i ni," magistrate chuan ring deuhvin a ti a, "Semyon, la bo rawh u!</p>
<p>Tun hma chuan in kan sak hian dâp chhuat kan hmang thin.</p>
<p>Hei mâi hrui hi i ei dawn nia.</p>
<p>English-ho pawh hian an chenna ram thliarkar hi a zim em aṭangin, anmahni thawnthu ngawt chuan a daih seng lo a ni ang, an thliarkar pawna mi chengte chanchin, Greek literature leh hman lai thawnthu te chu, an thu leh hla ziak nan subject-ah an hmang nasa em em a. Marlow-a ziak Doctor Faustus te, Milton-a poetry, Paradise Lost te, Shelley-a thu ziak Prometheus Unbound te, Keats-a kut chhuak, Ode on a Grecian Urn te, Tennyson-a ziak Ulesses te, James Joyce-a ziak Ulysses te leh Shakespeare-a kut chhuak tam takah Greek-ho thawnthu lch an literature lam thil chhuidawn tur tam tak kan hmu a English literature hi Greek thawnthu leh literature-in a chiah hnch nasatzia hi hriat sen leh chhuichhuah sen loh khawp a ni.</p>
<p>An khawngaihthlâk êm êm, nasa tak mai an thi a, nula tam tak chuan mittui hul thei lovin Lentlang an liam an tih kha. Chúng thi ve ta lo vânneite zingah chuan vânduai êm êmin Thanghniangi lo tel ve a, kum rei tak khawchak Pawi zingah a han tâng ta a ni. In lamah Chalkunga lah chuan lunglêng êm êmin, mittui nên, an sûlhnute a lo fang thin a. Sava veh tum hlek lovin sairawkherh leh saihlum nên a chhuak thin. A tâwpah chuan buhfai tukkhum tawngin a phur a, Thanghniangi zawng tûrin tuipui ràl a kai ta a.</p>
<p>Khua chu a nghâk thim a. Rei tak kea a kal avângin a keartui a na hle a; chuvang chuan dingdihlip deuh aih aihin a kal ta a. Darkar khat hnu velah lawngpâr zuartu dawr chu a va thleng a. Tukverh thir kham kâr aṭanga Najab-an zawi dam raiha a koh chuan, Fatimah-i chu sakhi hlau zuang zawk ang hian a tho vat a. Najab-a a ni em tih a han ngaihtuah leh rih phawt a. Kawng a va hawn chuan lâwm avângin a hmêl chu a êng phât mai.</p>
<p>Kan chhûngkaw pawna mi tih ni theiin i ring em?</p>
<p>Hei hi min tihsak ta che.</p>
<p>Mipain hmeichhia a biakin a biangah chibai bukna fawh thianghlim a tih dawnin a lukhum a la thla ngei ngei tur a ni. Bianga infawh hi hnam dang leh ram changkangho inchibai dan a ni. Mizote pawh hian kan uar ṭan ve sawt hle a ni.</p>
<p>Naupangten an sawi duh leh an rilrua thu awmte chu ngaihnawm tak leh indawt fel taka mite rilru hnch thei tur ang zawnga an ziak thiam theih nan. Hetah hi chuan tawngkaa sawi chhuak nghal mai lovin lehkhaah an thuphuah chu an ziak dawn a ni.</p>
<p>Parbawr te hi var sar tura kan duh chuan maida tlem thlâkin a rawng a tidanglam lova a tha ve khawp mai.</p>
<p>Ni e, Zuitei pa, engah nge maw i hmanhmawh viau thin le? Ti rawh u, thu ve rih rawh u. Kha thutthleng a awm kha.</p>
<p>Hetianga thil a lo awm hi a danglam hle. Paletwa khuaa inbengbel Church of England kohhranah te leh Chin Hills hmar lam khaw hrang hrangah te harsatna engmah a awm lo a. Mindat bial Hambon khuaah te pawh Buddhist Puithiam tan in an sa a, engmah harsatna an tawk bawk lo.</p>
<p>E thu teh u khai. Meizuk te ka'n siam ang che u. A hranin in lo chuangkai ngai si lo.</p>
<p>Pi Riali chuan, "/ van ngaihtuah thiam ve Chala. Chutiang ngaihtuah nachâng ka hre ve hlei nem. Thangbawnga chu lo ni hlauh se kan va ti ve maw aw, Chala! A pa te chu lo haw thuai thuai se kan va ti ve maw le," a ti a, a beng a chhi deuh reng mai a.</p>
<p>Kan han kal leh hlek a, chawlh-hmun titih remchang tak 'thingse-tui an tihah chuan anni pawh an phur nghat meuhin kan chawl tlâng a. Tui te ina hmai te kan phih thlan-daih deuh hnu chuan kal zai rêlin kan inthen dâwn ta a.</p>
<p>Tunah chuan kan Mizoram University-ah pawh Women Studies Department a lo ding ta hial a, a tihzia hle mai. Hmeichhe dinhmun chhui leh zirzauna te, anmahni tanpui, veng leh thuamchak zawnga ke penna chi hrang hrang a awm chho reng bawk. Tunah hian H. Lalngurliani chanchin leh chhehvel bakah a thawnthu ziak pahnihte hmun khatah kan rawn chhawp chhuah aṭang hian, eng thil emaw zir chhuah tur a awm ngei ang le.</p>
<p>Sanga pawh chu reiloteah chuan an bunna lam pan chuan a peng ve ta a. A pen dawn chuan, "Kei pawh Chawlhni dawnah ka lo haw vein ka inring. Ka niin zu a sak a thlum tawh e, i rui phel phawk dawn nia, zu alawm i duh ber ni!" a han ti hmak a.</p>
<p>Khawzima awmho Raltête chuan Chawhte khua an rawka, darbu an laksak a. An hausak aṭangin dar hmingthang tak tak Siallam dar te, Selbuang dar te, Tuaichawng dar te leh Liando dar te sum leh paiin an lei khawm a, Khawzima Ralteho kutah a lut vekin an sawi.¹</p>
<p>Hmingtha Chawnglunga chuan;</p>
<p>Aw, ka nau, Kristian pawh in la ni lo a va awm ve aw! Sande sikul pawh i hre lo maw? Biak in tinah a awm alawm. Zawng ula, naktukah kal ngei ngei ang che u. Hei, pawisa ka pe ang che. In ei tur lei ula, haw leh rawh u. Hetiang khawlai mai maiah in zawng hmu lo vang.</p>
<p>Thang leh thar nun sang zelah hian,</p>
<p>Kan awmna kha Sazek ngawpui niin, lehkhabu tha kan dapna kha kan tawmna bûk aṭanga ni thum kal zet Chittagong ni mah sela, miin a tum tlat chuan lehkhabu tha leh magazine ṭangkai chin chu chhiar tûr a nei reng thin a ni. Kan sawi tawh lehkhabu tha ka chhiarte kha tûn dinhmun kan thlen huna kan hma lam thlir dân tûr fuh leh kawng dik kan zawh theihna tûr atâna thil pawimawh leh ṭangkai tak a lo ni reng mai. MNF Sorkar kha sorkar te reuh tê, chak lo tak, Pakistan ISI châwm hlâwm ni mah ila, khatih hun laia International Relations chak deuh maia danglam khân min nghawng na ber a, kan têt avâng leh kan chak loh avâng tak khân kan duh ang zâwngin India Sub-Continent Politics lo danglamna chu, kan tâna tha tûr zâwnga her danglam tûrin thiltihtheihna leh chakna kan nei der si lo a. Chuvang tak chuan kan tân chuan inchhiar zau ngun a ngai lehzual a ni.</p>
<p>Rokimi a tap bawk, Ramhluni tap bawk. Chu hla an sa zo chu tah aw teuh chung hian Ramhluni chuan hmana buai tirha an khaw hlui Biak-ina Volunteer pakhat thu sawitu-in a thlan, Rozuala khawthlang lama a zin dawn aṭanga lunglëng taka a sak, "'Thihna Jordan kamah lungngaihin thla a zár' tih kha ka'n thlang ve ang e aw," a ti a. Chu hla an han sa zet phei chu an thian tak tak a: 'Lawmna kawl êng tur chu tapin ka thlir nilèn, Hmuh ni awm ang maw, ngaih a nâ e Lalpa; Ka tân khua vartir leh ang che, Aw, tah lai ka bang ve tawh ang,' 'Ka chènna tûr ram nuam ka ngai khawvelah hian, Tah chuan Lalnunnem pâr tlânin zai an sa; Bâng lovin Saron pâr an thliak, Ka thlir lungngaih hnuaiah hian,' tih an sak chhûng zawng chuan a súma insûm rual loh lungchhiatna chuan Ramhluni chu a rawn hnawh leh ta a.</p>
<p>Thinrim thei lo mihring hi tumah an awm tak tak lo vang.</p>
<p>Mama nu, harh rawh, tho teh, i va chau awm ve, engtinnge ka awm leh pek a? Thil awm dan ka va chiang lo em. Engti laiin nge ka thawmhnawte chu ka lo thlâk reng reng chu le. Ka chauin ka ril a tam hle mai, a remchan chuan chaw ei min han siam ta che, ka'n inphih harh dawn ang e.</p>
<p>Perek then khat ber dan hi chu duhthua sâm tlat lo.</p>
<p>Fimkhur ula, in hleh bulh lutuk chuan a nâ ang.</p>
<p>Lo inhawng rawh Salem khawpui.</p>
<p>Kan pi leh pute'na an thawnthu min hnutchhiah, CHEMTATRAWTA kha kan va inhmeh tehlul em! Kha thawnthu kha nuihpui chungin kan tu leh fate kan hrilh chhawng zel a, Zofa zingah hre lo alawi kan awm lo ang. Kha thawnthu aṭanga zir chhuah tur kan neih hi tun hun, harsatna kan tawh lai hian ngaihtuah chhuah a va ṭul em! Pitarte tuikhur hnara lo daikal kha, a huatthlalakna em em chu an khaw tui tlan a tibawlhhlawh kha a ni ber ang. Mipui rorelnaah khan a pawimawh hmasa ni ta ber chu, kha hmuna a daikal chhan zawn chhuah kha a ni. Tichuan, an chhuiin an zawng zel a, a tawpah chuan Chemtatrawta chem tat lai lo cheptu kaikuang chalah phung a tawp ta a. A mawhphurtu kaikuang khan eng nge a sawi? "Meia min rawh leh ka sen vit vet ang a, tuia min chiah leh ka dang bim bem ang," tih mai kha a ni. Tichuan, meiah an rawh a, a sen vet vet a, tuiah an vawm lut a, "Pi leh pute khua chu nuam singkhaw," tiin a hleuh kual ta zak zak mai a, thawnthu a tawp der!</p>
<p>Amaherawhchu, khing khi determiner, pahnih tih leh second personal pronoun nang/nangmah tih nen a inkawp thei lo thung. Nang nena chen za ka duh. Kan pahnihin kal ho ang. Hetiang hian khing thumalte khi a inkawp rem ve thei lo. Nang tih khi second personal singular pronoun a ni a, mi pakhat chauh sawina a ni. Pahnih tih pawh khian adverb kawppui tur atan dun a hman a ngai. Hetiang hian:</p>
<p>Tomato hring la hel deuh chu a hmin that theih nan apple hmin leh tomato hmin sa te nen lehkha ip phui takah tuam la, polythene bag vit pawpin tuam la, a ti hmin tha ve duh khawp mai. Tin, chutiang bawkin balhla hel tih hmin i duh chuan balhla hmin tawh te nen tuam la, kar lovah a hmin ve mai.</p>
<p>Khua a lo thal a, Sechhun tur leh Chawng tur hi an awm deuh thluah a, nula leh tlangval te chu an hlim hle hlawm thin. Sathing zara a ruala thing phurh dual dual te a lo awm tan a. Chalkunga pawh hmeithai fa mah ni se, tlangval chak pawl leh tlawmngaia taima pawl a ni a, a lar ve hle a, nuam chu a ti ve em em a. Thanghniangi nen thu tiam an neih chinah phei chuan ngaih thatna tak a neih aṭangin a rilru chu a engthawl ve em emani. Darpuia'n khuang a chawi dawn a, chawng buh dengin nula rual leh tlangval rual chu zan tin an ri tlut tlut mai thin a, mite chu an hlim em em a. Sathing zara thing phurh te an awm a, nula leh tlangval chu an awl hman mang lo. A ni a lo thleng a, chawng an han chen leh a, sumdeng zu te an in a, tlangvalho chuan nuam an ti em em mai a. Sumdeng zu ina chawng chennaah te chuan mahni ngaihzawngte kher kha lampui theih a lo ni bik lo va. Chalkunga leh Thanghniangi te pawh an intawng zeuh zeuh zel bawk nachungin, hetih ni hian chuan, an duhthusam angin an awm thei bik thin lo a ni.</p>
<p>A hmel chu a tha khawp mai, mahse a lerh deuh a ni.</p>
<p>Enga ti nge ka farnu Awfeli mangang reng renga i siam fo ni? Lal fapa pawh ni la, i duh duh i tithei bik lo ve aw. Hmangaih leh duat takin i farnu ka lo enkawlsak lai che a, chutia mi han tih vei chu le? I duh em ni? Sawi rawh. I farnu Awfeli chu awm lo se mual i liam nghal a ni mai, i hria em? Tu nge ka nih i hre na nge?</p>
<p>Sial khaw bawar Emaw, pau thei lo.</p>
<p>Mi hrang hrang siam Mizo tawng grammar bû tha tak tak kan nei ve nual tawh a; chuti chung chuan kei teh lul hi mi thiam ril zâwk nia ka ngaihte'na Mizo tawng kalphung mil ngei grammar bû siam tura mi an ngen der ve tâk si-ah chuan, insit tak chungin he lehkhabû hi ka rawn chhawp chhuak ve ta râwih mai a ni. A tirah chûan grammar term hrang hrang sawi fiahna bâkah hian, Mizo tawngin kalphung danglam bik a neihna lãi leh, a ziah dân thû-ah pawh grammar kalphung hran a neih dân sawi fiahna te, grammar aṭanga Mizo tawng thumal hrang hrang chipchiar zâwka bih chianna te telh tumin ka ziak zet tawh a; amaherawhchu, chúng zawng zawng chu bu khata beng khâwm a nih chûan phêk za ruk lâia chhah a ni dâwn ta mai a. Chuvàngin, mi thil hre zâwkte'na thu mi an ràwn angin, bu khat tura ruahman tawh kha bu hnih atân ka then hrang leh a; grammar bu pangngaia dah àwm chin nia lang kha he lehkhabu-ah hian ka rawn khung khâwm hmasa ta a. Tichuan, he lehkhabûa dah luh ve tâk loh, grammar aṭanga chipchiar zâwka Mizo tawng bih chianna thu dang chu bu hrana rawn tih chhuah leh zâi ka rêl ta zâwk a ni.</p>
<p>Naupang thanlen zel dan leh tawng an thiam chhoh dan inlaichinna chik taka thil zirtu (researcher)-te hmuh dan leh nangma hriat ve dan aṭangin sawi fiah teh.</p>
<p>Israel fate hi anmahni ram aṭanga Rome roreltute'n an um chhuah hnuah khawvel ram tinah an darh a. An pem luhna ramah tihduhdah an ni zui a. Britain-ah ngei pawh Israel mi pem lutte'n harsatna tam tak an tawk thin. Mahse, khawvel sawrkar lian dangte'n Israel fate tana an tih ve nia lang hauh lo, British sawrkar chauhvin an tih nia lang a awm a. Pathianin chhechham meuhva an ram tura a pek nia an ngaih Palestine ram chu Israel-te lung tilengtu ber a ni. Khawvel sawrkar chak ber chu British-ho an nih laiin Israel fate Palestine rama an kir leh theihna tur dar chu Britain aṭangin a lo ri a. Chu chu November 2, 1917 kuma British Foreign Secretary Arthur James Balfour hnen aṭanga thuchhuak a ni. Hei hi Balfour Declaration tih hial khawpa hmingthang a ni a. Juda mi hruaitu pakhat hnena lehkha a thawnah Palestine rama Judate tan ram din thar leh hi British sawrkar ngaih dan a ni ti ang deuhvin lehkhaah hian dah a ni. He lehkhathawn hian Judate tana Palestine-a anmahni ram ngei an din thar leh thuah ṭangkaina nasa tak a nei ta a ni.</p>
<p>A danglam thin thu kan sawi mêk na a, danglam ve ngai lo aṭangin a bul ṭan ila, a chiang thei deuh awm e. Thumal chu mood hrang hranga hman pawha a lam rik dan leh a sipel danglam ve chuang ngai lo a han awm phawt a.</p>
<p>Rei rial lovin Tachhipho chuan Hmawngkawn lal Lungliana chu Buangtheuva khawper Ruanzawl rûnpui ah an zuk sâwm a. Tichuan Ruanzawl rûn tûr chuan Tachhip leh Hmawngkawn chu an kal ta a. Tachhipho chu Thangzika Hauhnar leh Tumtawia hovin an kal a. Tachhip tlangvâl ṭhenkhat chu Hmunpuiho an ûmnaah an intihsual hlawm avângin an kal lo va, Khuangluta pawh a fung palna a ke a la vûn ûl avângin a kal lo va.</p>
<p>Tin, Lehkha emaw, napkin paper thil huh hip thei chi hi i fridge mawngah khan dah la, hnah duk thei chu a duk tur a veng ve thei a ni. I thil napkin phah te chuan tuihu chhuak tam lutuk te a lo hip khawl ang a, thlai rah chhe thei pawh rei tak a vawng tha thei a ni. Tin, sponge te pawh thil huh hip tur chuan a tha hle bawk a ni.</p>
<p>Sa thau mawm hi kawr leh puanah a kai chuan khawnvartui -a sil hmasak a, chumi hnuah insuk sahbawnin suk a, nisaah pho leh mai tur a ni. Ni sa chuan mawm chu a hip bo mai. Puan leh kawr chu i la su ui deuh a nih chuan a kai laiah khan powder dip han tal tlawrh la, ni hnih ni thum velah hnuah su la, mawm chu a reh ve thei a ni. Tin, methylated spirit lapuaa chiahin a fai tha thei bawk.</p>
<p>Mizorama high school naupangte mizo tawng zirtir nana lehkhabu hman mekte sawi la, hengho hi a thatna leh that tawk lohna sawiin a siam that dan tur rawtna siam nghal rawh.</p>
<p>Tawng leh hnam nun phung hian inzawmna a neih vek aṭangin, tawng kalhmang leh awmzia hre chiang tur chuan a zawmpui leh a lo chhuahna hnam nun phung chu hriat a ngai a. Sapho fiamthu ṭhenkhat lehkhabua ziak kan chhiar thina kan nuih a zat vak thin lohna chhan pawh hi an nun phung leh kan nun phung a inan loh vang a ni a, an fiamthu thawhna ṭawngkam chuan kan rilruah thu a sawi ve lo a ni. Mizo fiamthuah pawh Sapho lo nuih vena tur a awm lo fo bawk. Hnam nun phung leh rilru hi grammar leh dictionary aṭang mai chuan zir thiam sen a ni lo. Tawng ri bakah kan thu sawi laía kan hmel lan dan, kan mit men dan te, kan hmui siam danglam dan te, kan lu leh koki tihchet dan leh ban vai dante pawh hi entir tam tak nei thei. chetziaa thu sawina a ni a, tawng zir mite chuan an ngai pawimwh em em a ni. Miin hnam dang tawng a zirin pianpui tawnga hmangtute hnam nun phung hriatna lamah hma a sawn chak dan ang zelin chu hnam tawng chu a thiam chak ve zel dawn a ni tih hi tawng zir chungchang thua mi thiamte ngaihdan a ni. Hnam nun phung leh rilru put dan hriatna nei si lova hnam dang tawng miin a lo hman chuan, Rousseau-an a sawi angin, mi pakhatin French tawng ringawt pawh hi tawng hrang paruk laiah a chantir thei mai dawn a lo ni. Mizo tawng hmangtu ṭhenkhat hian kan tawnga thu mal ṭhenkhat tlawmngaihna tih ang te hi Sap tawngah pawh a awm ve lo ve tih changchawiin Mizo tawng hi hausa ta luaah kan ngai a ni mai thei. Tawng tinah hian hnam dang tawnga lehlin fiah that theih loh thu tam tak a awm vek a ni. Sap tawng thu mal tam tak, Mizo tawnga lehlin ngaihna kan hriat loh aṭanga kan tawng ang maia kan hman tam tawhziate hi ngaihtuahin kan tawng hi Sap tawng aiin a hausak zawk a rinawm lo hle a ni. Mizo zinga mi thiam hmasa pawl Pastor Liangkhaian Mizote hi hla thua kan hausakzia a sawinaah, Mizo hian hla thu bik kan nei nasa em em mai a, Saphote ai chuan kan ngah daih awm e. a lo tih te pawh hi a fiahna awm ang kan la hmuh loh aṭangin, a ngial a ngana pawm mai a har a ni.</p>
<p>A lo nui ki leh vun vun a. Ka lehlinna lehkha chu en pawh en mang lo hian a zial tawp tawp a, min pe lêt a.</p>
<p>A summary a pe thei ang, a remkhawm thiam ang, sawihonaah a sawi ve thei ang, thu tlukna a siam thei ang, a zir thu laimu a sawi/ziak thei ang, a tlangpui a sawi thei ang etc.</p>
<p>Puithiam chu a ngawi vung vung a, 'Chutiang hming a awin ngai lo. Lana a ni lovang, Rana a ni ang, a ti a. Chutih lai chuan naupang chu a lo harh a, khawnvar eng hnuaiah chuan puithiam hmai rang rek ruk leh a zirtir hmai rangho chu an lo thu khup mai a. Naupang hlau lutuk mangang chu zun a duh a, 'Ka zung, a ti a, tuman a awmzia chu an hre lo va. Puithiam chuan chemte a keng a, naupang chu a'n en a, 'Tu nge? a han ti a. Naupang hlau lutuk chuan a lu a bu ringawt a, chu chu 'Aw' a tihnaah an ngai a. Puithiam chu a phun sup sup a. Puithiam rilruah chuan mak takin hlauhna a awm a, a zep hram hram a. Mahse, chemte a han lak chuan, a inthup zo lo va. a khur chhuak ta a. Lal-Ra, Rana-Jung. Ni lo, ni lo. Lal Ram Jung-Jung Ha!' a ti a, aw tial ruatin a au chhuak ta a.</p>
<p>Kha kha eng ngati nge?</p>
<p>Ennawm chhuahnaah a entuin chhuah ve ngai a ni tih an hre lo ang bawka thil tih kawng tinrênga tel ve ka tum lo chu ka thiam lo a ni. Mahse chhuanlam pakhat ka nei a ni. Chumi avâng chuan thil tih chu sawi loh, mumang neih takngial pawh theih ni se khapsak min duh a ni a. Chuvângin eng mah hi ka ṭânghma ah kai lovin ka rål thlîr vek mai a ni. In satuin in ropui tak a rel a, zan khat thlipui a lo thawk a, a tihchhiatsak vek a, eng mah lovah a chang zo taṭangin, ka rilru ka suangtuahna leh ka ruat zawng zawng chu tihchhiatin a awm zo ta. Tûnah hian thufing pakhat, "Mihringin a ruat a, Pathianin a thiatsak a," tih hi a dik tih ka lo hre chhuak ta. Thil ropui tak tak tih kan tumin kan ngaihtuah vêl a, mahse Pathianin a duh duhin a thiat leh thei a ni. Chuvângin kan suangtuah leh kan duhthusâmte hi a tak a lo thien hma loh chuan kan ringin inhnem nân kan hmang mai tùr a ni lo. Vawiin aṭangin naktûka awm dân tûr kan hre lo. Engti anga nasa pawhin ngaihtuah ila, kan dung hi tawng khat pawhin kan puntir thei bawk hek lo. Hêngte hi ka ngaihtuah laiin ka rilruah he hla hi a lo chhuak a ni.</p>
<p>Lallula thlah zinga Lalsavunga fapa Vanhnuailiana chu chhak nawr turin, a thlang tlak hnuah khawchhak a pan leh a, tlang hrang hrang a zuan hnuin Champhai a thleng a, Tiau chhak lam aṭanga Mizoram rawn tibuai fotute nek a duh vang a ni pakhat a, chu chu hlain a hril a:</p>
<p>Ka lo hlauthâwng hman teh asin.</p>
<p>Awi ka rei! U Sanga chu a va ngaihtuahawm ve! Chu an zawng em ni?</p>
<p>Hawh u, he sakei lu hi a chhe sawm deuh vek tawh si a, kan pi pute tih danin, A aitu kawtah hian Seluphan phun ila, a sa lu dang saw tha deuhin i tarsak ang u.</p>
<p>A rawn bihthla dâk dâk a.</p>
<p>IDENTITY khat nei an nihzia tichiang tura Mizo hnahthlâk zawng zawngten tobul thuhmun sawi tur an neih dan te, pi leh pu aṭanga sulhnu hriatreng tlak an neihho dan te, Culture lama zaikhata luang an nih dan te, hmaṭang aṭanga chhuahna hmunkhat nei an nih dan te, tawng inang tam tak an neih aṭanga eng hunah emaw chuan khawsaho an lo nih tawh dan te, inan tlanna leh inhnaih riauna an neihho dan te chu sawi ngai loah dah ila.</p>
<p>Taksa chetna lam chiah a rualpuite tih ang a ti ve thei em/thei lo em record tur.</p>
<p>Pi leh pu aṭang tawhin Mizote hi chaw atâna buh-chang ring hnam leh mahni kutkawiha inchâwm an nih avângin thlawhhma lâk an ulukin an fimkhur êm êm a. Lo nghet nei lova kum tina ngawpui vâta lo thar din zêla buh leh bâl chinga ei-zawng an ni a. Chaw tihduhdah leh tihnawmnah chu thil thiang lo, buh leh bâl mit lohna leh thlawhhma lama hmuingil lohna thila an ngaih avângin chawei bâng fahran pawh an tiduhdah ngam ngai lo. Tin, buh-chang chauh hi chaw-a an ngaih avângin a dang zawng chu chaw-chhia ani a. Chuvângin, 'chaw-chhia-ah chuan tai a tui ber' an ti thin. Miin buh-chang a tlâkchham chuan ei nei lo leh ṭâm an ni a. Mualpho tâwpkhâwk a nih avângin ei neih tumin ṭan an la nasa ngiang rêng thin. Kum tina an lo neih an sawn ziah thin avângin Mizo thlawhhma lâk dân hi a hahthlâk a, a bulah an tan kum tin mai a ni.</p>
<p>Cable TV kal tlanga buatsaih reality show lar tak tak pathum: Talent Search, Look Alike Contest leh Comedian Search-ah te Chief Judge/Judge a lo ni tawh thin. Mafa-a kha zirna ina thawk ni lo mah se a thu ziakte hian mi a hneh theih em aṭangin thangtharte zinga thu leh hlaa tuina leh phurna tuhtu leh ziakmi tam tak hringtu a ni a tih theih awm e. A kutchhuakte hi luhchilha, zirbing chak tak tak thalaite zingah an thahnem hle niin a lang. Thangtharte zinga thu leh hla thiam, a kut chhuak tam tak hmanga chhiartute lo awi tlei a, lo awi lungleng thintu Mafa- a Hauhnar chuan kum 42 mi lek niin ni 30 December, 2018 Pathianni zing dar 5 khan chatuan ram a lo pan ta a ni.</p>
<p>Plural form 'tc, etc.,' hi adjective/adverb-ah kan beitir thin a, hei hian kan sawi tum tihfiah loh a nei fo. Kan qualify-tur duh chuan a noun kha a ni si a, 'Kei grep hrui tak tak ka ni' tih hi Mizo tawng dik tak chu a ni a, mahse thangthar rilruah 'tak tak hian hrui qualify zawkin a lang a ni awm e, grep hi a qualify tak chu a ni si a. Hetiang thilah hian a grammar dik ngawt aiin hriat fuh theih tura sawi tum a tha fo zawk awm e.</p>
<p>Vawk no, ui no' tia sawi an phal loh lâia, 'vawkte, uite ti chauha sawi an phal chungchângah hian nichina kan sawi, phêk 92-naa 'te' leh 'no' -te hi an nihna hre fuh lova, 'vawkte tia ziah zawm ve tur emaw an tih ang bawka 'bâwngno' tia ziah zawm tur emaw an tih kha han sawi zui ila: 'no' hi chu common noun thu mal, mahnia mal din thei a nih dan kha kan târ lang tawh a. Chutih lajin 'te' erawh hi chu noun nena kan sawi kawpnaah mahnia a mal din ve dâwn chuan adjective a ni daih thin a ; chuvangin, 'no anga noun thu mal a nih ve loh aṭangin ziah hran ve chi a ni lo a, 'no' nen hian a ziah dan turah a inanga hrùt pawp chi a ni lo hrim hrim mai a ni.</p>
<p>Common noun thu mal 'bûr' pawh a kawppui thu dang nena ziah dan turah, tun hmâ aṭanga 'bûr' kan lo neih tawh thin chu culture nen inzawm bikah an ngâi a, "Tun hmâ aṭanga 'bûr' hran bika kan lo neih tawh a ni a, zawm ni se," tiin 'chingalthlawrbûr, saumbûr.adt.' tia ziah zawm tur an ti a. Tun hnua 'bûr' kan neihho erawh chu culture nen a inzawm ve lovah an ngâi ni tur a ni, "'Bûr' dang erawh chu ziah hran zel ni se," an ti a, 'chi bûr, chini bûr, thingpuife bûr.adt.' tiin a inzawm lova ziah tur an ti thung leh bawk a.</p>
<p>I ah that loh chuan i thlauh bo palh ang e.</p>
<p>Tun hma chuan, ram huan pal hrûlah lei an rût khuar zui thin.</p>
<p>A thlungluah rawn vuan che,</p>
<p>Washing powder fiante 4-5 vel dettol chhin hnih leh tui no 2 vel pawlhin leih den den la, emaw spray na i neih chuan sprayna burin spray laṭangin a tha ve tho a ni.</p>
<p>Puithiam leh Pastor-te hian Lalpa zanriah sacrament hi khûn tak leh urhsun takin an buatsaih thin.</p>
<p>Sawn pek e maw le, ka huphurh tak tak a. Mi ta chhiar hawh a nih aṭangin tlem tlem a ziak chhawng a ngai si a, kan Sikul hian engtin nge min hriatthiam theih dawn a ni le, zir tur neih loh te tan chuan a huphurhawm khawp mai.</p>
<p>Ram huanah ran an luh loh nân dâi an thêu thin.</p>
<p>Malsawmi a thi maw? Ka ring thei lo. A mak em mai.</p>
<p>Ani hi zawng mi a chhan hneh thei a nia. A che reng hi a rang mai a.</p>
<p>Miin ramsial leh sai ni lo, sa serh kai chin kap ta se, a tluk hmun thleng hmasaber chuan a bawp a man ang a. A kahna silai chu ama silai a nih chuan, a dar veilam lal sachhuah tur tih loh, a dar dinglam leh a bawp pahnih chu a bawp mantuten an chang ang. Mahse thian dun chauh an nih chuan a thianpa-in a bawp a man hnu-ah a kap tu chanvo baka lal sadar leh khawlaisa tur bak chu zah leh zahin an insem tawh mai thin. A kaptu chan chu: Angum, a ir no, a lu, a lung, a zangti thlur leha pumpui sutute chanvo ang chan khat leh tlang sa chan khat ang a chang thin a. Mi an tam deuha a bawp mantu tur awm chuang lo a nih chuan, a kaptu-in, "Mai chan barh ila, kan insem tlang dawn nia," a tih chuan sa serh pek tur leh a kaptu chan bak chu an mai chan bawk thin a ni. San an kaha an chan fel hnu-a an hawn dawnin an sa chan chhan hnahchhawl reng reng chu an paih darh leh vek zel a, chu chu 'chhawl tho' an ti a. chutia an tih kher nachhan chu an thil duh loh zawngin an sulhnu chu rawn chhuiin an chung eng thil thal lo emaw thlen phah theiha an ngaih vang a ni. An haw dawna an hnuhnung berin an thla chu ramah a cham bang ang tih hlua-in, 'Kan hawng e aw,' tiin a sawm ngai ngei tur a ni bawk.</p>
<p>Tukthuan kan ei fel a, ka nu leh ka pute an kal hma chuan ka pu (ka pa pa) chu a ṭawngṭai a. An kal tûr an inphurh hnu chuan ka nu chuan, "Bawihte, kawtchhuah thleng chauh talin min thlah ta che. Ka va han ngai dâwn tehlul che êm," a ti a. Mahse ka pate-a chuan, "Thlah lo ang, in lung a lêng lutuk ang. Ti hian kawtkaiah kan inchibai ang a tawk rawh se. Eng chen pawh kal se inthlâkhlelhin tawpintai a nei chuang lo ang," a ti tlat mai a. Ka nute chu an inphur a, kawtkaiah chuan kan inchibai den den a. Mahse kei chuan ka nu chu ka chibai thei thlâwt lo. An kal liam dawn têpa ka nu rawn lehhawi lehin tap râwl teuha, "Bawihte, ka va ngai dawn tehlul che êm! Vawi khat chauh i biang ka'n fawp leh teh ang," tiin a rawn kîr leh hrâm hrâm a. Kawtkaiah chuan phurrit tawk phur chungin ka biangah chuan min han fåwp vawng vawng a.</p>
<p>In puanzar leh palha ka ngûnhnâm laka tuar huam chung ranin tuna kan thil hmuh hi tu hnen maha puangzar lo turin chhia chham rawh u.</p>
<p>Fá chu 'buh' tihna a ni a. Buh kûng a lo no va, a lo duah that theihna tûra buh malsawmna tûra sakhaw hmanna a ni a. Pi leh pute chu thlawhhma la-a ei zawng vek an nih avângin buh bål malsâwmna an mamawh êm êm a. Buh leh bâl a hlâwk theihna tûra khawtlâng hun pawimawh a nih avângin an ngai pawimawh lo thei lo a. Khawtlâng huap sakhaw hmanna a nih avângin khawtlâng neitu lal inah an hmang thin a. Khaw chhûng mi tumah chhuak-vâk awm lovin awmni an kham a. Dân pângngai angin a Bawlpu leh a thawitu ber chu Sadawt a ni a. A thawina tûr, pa neinung deuhin âr an thawh chu Sadawtin a talh dawnin lal tapai lamah thu-in heti hian a han chham a:</p>
<p>Lersia hnenah vawiin hian buh in chil dawn leh silai zâwn dah theihna thlâm leh hrui in nei tih i hrilh a ni lawm ni?</p>
<p>Vai tawng pawh hi kan hmang nasa. Kan tawnga kan neih hmiah pawh a tam mai. Chabi, kawlawm, sap, hmarcha, alaichi, pan, mawza, kamis, sana leh a dang tam tak, kan tawng an tíhausa sawt. Sap tawng pawh, vai tawng pawh kan tawnga kan neih tâk hmiahte hi chu an thain kan tawng an tihausa a, a lawmawm hle. Mahse, kan ṭawngkam awm sa kan lantir chuan kan tawngin a pachhiat phah ve thung ang a, a pawi lam hret ang. Kan tawnga kan hman nghal pawh ni lo, kan ṭawngkam lántu pawh ni lem lo, Saptawng thiamin an hman ve hrim hrim a awm a. Saptawng thiam lem lo pawhin an hmang ve a; nichina tumbu zuarho hman ang chi te kha mihlim tawnghriat loh lamah Saptawng kan telh a, mihlim pakhat tawnghriat loh pawh Saptawng hlirin a tawng e an tih vangin, Saptawng thiamin an han ngaihthlâk nâk chuan eveready hongkong a lo ti zaih zaih mai nia. Amah upa tawng takin, ka naupan laiin kei pawhin ka hre ve a, nula tleirawl tê hian a tawnghriatloh-ah chuan, Holis, the king holis a ti zat zat mai a ni. Hnam dang tawng hi, tawng hriatah leh tawnghriatlohvah pawh kan tih phung a ni ve rêng rêng a ni ang e. Kan ngaihtuah fo tur chu, kan tawng a tihausa nge a tipachhia tih hi a ni.</p>
<p>A dik a dawk pawh thlu hlei lo hian a âng buan buan leh ngawt zel a!</p>
<p>Good morining. Please sit down. This time only five of you passed in first division. Zoduhawma stood first. Where is he? What about your friend Ralliana? He's absent for a week.</p>
<p>Nuih pawh nui thê thâw suh u, min rawn kaitho vat ula, a ni mai!</p>
<p>Vâla, tunlai chu i cher theû tho riau mai, a tha lam nge tha lo lam?</p>
<p>A hmel a tha i ti mai nge i hmangaih tak tak? Hmangaihna hi chatuan entirna a ni, an ti a;</p>
<p>Savun bâwl hi a khât tawka eiah chuan chawhmeh tui tak a ni ve.</p>
<p>Engtikah nge i chhuah dawn?</p>
<p>E le, mipa.awh hmeichhia, khawi maw han sawi tha hle hle teh.</p>
<p>Radioactive nei thir rau rauah pawh a hlauhawm berte zinga mi, plutonium a lo nih vaih chuan keini khawih chi a ni lo tawp tih chu ka hre thiam ve reng mai. Engmah kan ti thei lo tlat a ni. Mi mal thila chhui vak chi ni pawhin a lang ta lo. Khawvel ram hausa leh thiltitheiten an zawn rawn, a tha lam emaw, tha lo lam emaw zawnga an hman ṭangkai em em a ni a, mi mala lo kawl veng veng chi lah a nih hmel ta lo tawp a. Lo la thei ta teh reng pawh ni ila fimkhur tawpa kawl ngai chi a ni a, a buaipuiawm dawn lutuk tih chu a lang reng mai a. A chinchang hre miah lova kawl phei chu a hlauhawm lehzual ngei ang. Ka pa khan a thil kawl kha eng nge a nih tih leh engtia mi dangin ngai pawimawh viau nge an nih ang tih lam kha a hre chak ve hlein ka ring a. Khati taka hlu nia a hriat lung kha kan khuaah hian a keng lut ang a, an chuh buai reng bawk si aṭangin thuhrukna tur a zawng ta a nih ka ring. Thawnthua a lan dan nen han khaikhinin a tikeh palh a ni ngei ang. Mahse, a han en chiang ang a, a han lek kang vel ang a, chu thir chu amahin a lo sa ringawt ang a. Radia- tion hlauhawmzia a hre âwm der si lo va, kut lâwngte khan a keng mai mai emaw a ni ang a! Ka ngaihtuah ang taka ti turah ka han dah chhin a, ka lainat lutuk!</p>
<p>Thenawm do a tha ngai lo. Râl do turin an kal. In an do tha. Chawndo niah rualin an do thin. A hmai a ser do mai. Mi rawn ban do do suh.</p>
<p>Ka remruat ang mi tâwmpui dâwn phawt chuan nang tak pawhin i la zahawm phah dâwn asin.</p>
<p>Tuan rel loin a leng zuar zuar e,</p>
<p>Saplala te hnutchhiah thuthlung kenkawh tumin an thuihruai Dara leh Satinkhara kha an lo kal leh a. Mahse, thawm thangva hmanga vauzam chi kan ni lo tih an hriatin, heh hilin an kir leh ta. Vai tirhkoh akara hnamchawm lehnghalin thu tha ka sawi e, an rawn ti chhen hi ka be peih lo viau a ni.</p>
<p>Hawrawp mal hawl kim ber leh lun ber tihtheih hian 'A' hi a danglam a, a awm lovin kawi khat mah kan ṭial hlei thei lo a nih ber mai. Mizo thu lam dana a thluk (^) peknaah hian 'a, aw, e, i, o, u' hman a ni thin a. He thluk pekna hi vawiin thleng hian kan la hmang thiam fumfe hlei thei lo chu a la nih ber hi. Thumal ṭhenkhat chu a thuziak hma leh hnu aṭanga fiah chawp a awm nual a, vawi khat chhiara mam thlarh pawh a awm thei bawk. Chuvangin, hriat thiamna durbin nena en rem mai hi a la tha rih zawk mai thei a ni. A thlukna siam chungchangah mi hrang hrangten an siam ve tawh nual nain an len tlak a la rual thei meuh lo. Mizo tawng ziah dan chungchangah pawh zawm tur leh zawm loh turah mahni style hman a la ni fan a. A hnu feah Mizo Language Committee-ten hma lain Mizoram Board of School Education hmingin 'Mizo Tawng Ziah Dan' tih bu an chhuah ta a. Hemi zul zui hian mi tam zawk chuan an rinchhan hle. Kan peng hla mah mah a, kir leh zawkin a hnukharna atan chuan 'A' hian khawi kipah pawh hlutna a neih nasatzia leh hawrawp mal din zinga awmzia a neih thahnemzia thu hi kan han tar lan duha chu a ni e.</p>
<p>Pa hâwkdâk deuh hi chu mipui awm khawmnaah hian an dâk uâu uâu zel!</p>
<p>Induh takin a vei ngâk ngâk a.</p>
<p>Thlipui na tak, thawnga-leivir tleh chu hlauhawm tak a ni.</p>
<p>Tichuan, Kawkpui chuan par ni a nei ta si lo va, anni pahnih pawh chu an lo inthen hlen ta a ni an ti.</p>
<p>Verb thu mala a beh thin bâkah verb leh adverb ṭang dunah te, transitive verb leh a object tang dunah te pawh a bet thin a. Verb leh adverb tang duna a beh chuan a behna thu inkawpte chu 'compounded verbal noun'-ah a siam a; chutiang bawkin transitive verb leh a object tang duna a beh pawhin a behna thu inkawpte chu 'compounded verbal noun'-ah a siam thin bawk a. Hei hi kan pûte hian grammar aṭanga hre fiah ve tawh si lovin, 'na' behna verb leh adverb te, 'na' behna transitive verb leh a object-te chu ziah dan phung mumal awm fel thei lo turin, a then an rawn ziah zawm a, a then an ziah zawm lo a; grammar-a nihna inang reng pawh ziah dan fel tak awm thei lo turin an rawn ching buarbuar ta vak mai a ni.</p>
<p>A va pangchang awm nghial nghual ve!</p>
<p>Rokimi chuan, "Keimah aṭanga hrehawm i tihna a nêp theih deuh dawn phawt chuan ka thlahthlam hauh lo ang che. Eng hunah pawh min mamawh chuan i lo kal hman loh leh inthlahrung hauh lovin min rawn kohtir mai thin dawn nia," a ti a, in an zuk thleng chu inleng an lo awm nual a.</p>
<p>Anniho hian lungrual takin thawh dan turte an ruahmanho zel a. Study Leave hial laa hnapui bera neiin Pu B. Lalthanglianan mawhphurhna a la a. Zoram chhûng leh State dangah te, India ram pawn lam thlengin an zin thin a. Member dangte hian a remchan dan angin an thawhpui zel bawk. Tin, lehkhabu thahnem tak chhiar a, rim taka inbuatsaih hnua a bua ziak chu Pu B. Lalthangliana koah Study Group hian mawhphurhna an pe a, a hah fal hle nghe nghe.</p>
<p>Bazarah ka kal a, sa ka lei. Bazarah ka kal a, sa ka lei a, ka kang a, ka ei ta a.</p>
<p>Thing kak nei sang deuh an phun a, chumi lerah chuan sakei ei duh zawng chi an tarh a, sakei lawn nan leilawn thing pahnih awn deuh de-dawin an dawh a, a hnuaiah fung an bun a. Sakei lawn chuan an tawktarh chu a pawt a, a pawh per veleh thing leilawn kha a chim ta thut a, a hnuaia an fung bun chuan a dulah a lo chhun ta thin a ni.</p>
<p>Kan tawng hi ri hlawm mal tawng a ni bawka, ri hlawm khat hi chu ziak zawm zel tur a ni. Mizo tawngah hawrawp lam rik loh kan nei ve lo. Khawlchhutah tlar tawpah thu sei deuh a lo awmin kan hai then a, a then lehlam chu tlar dawtah kan ziak thin. Ri hlawm khat chu hetianga then tur a ni ve lo. Mizo tawng hre lo khawlha remtute chuan a awmzia an hriat loh aṭangin an kai then thin, chhuang tih chu chhu-ang ti angin an kai then thin a, chhiar sual hlauhawm tak a ni. Ri hlawm ṭhenkhat chu ri dangin a zui chuan a rik dan a danglam thin a, khua chhía te chu khawchhete tiin kan lam a, chutianga ziak tur chu a ni. A ri danglam hì thu awm thiang a nih vanga danglam a nih chuan a tira a thlûk kha hman zel tur ti an awm a, ka ngaih dan chuan a awmna hmuna a rik dan ang angin a thlûk pawh kan chhinchhiah tur niin ka ring. Pa tih chu neitu sawina a nih chuan a ri sangin a sei a, pa pakhat tiha pa ri chu a tawiin a hniama. Chhiar sual theih awm chu Bible lehlin tharah a ri chungah emaw hnuaiah emaw a ri san leh hniam athu-in kan chhun.</p>
<p>I tan chauh aw kumtluangin.</p>
<p>Kan pi leh pute'n Khampat an chhuahsan lai hian tumna hmun bik pawh nei lova kal chhuak mai an nih hmel a, chhim lamah Sehawng khua awmna velah an chawl lawk phawt a ni awm e. Chuta tang chuan tlangramah an chho ta a, Thân Tlâng an liam hnuah Run lui an kan leh a. Tichuan, Run Lui chung lawkah hmun rem zawl tha tak an hmu a, chutah chuan khua dinin awmhmun an khuar ta a ni. Chu an khua chu an hotu ber Sumpuia hming chawiin, 'Sumpuihmun' an ti a ni. Sumpuihmun-a thangkhat lian zet an han awmkhawm hnuah chuan ram tha zuanin hmun hrang hrangah a hlawm hrante tein an kal chhuak ta zel hlawm a. Tichuan, zawi zawiin Run leh ṭiau inkar hmun tinah an lo inzardarh ta a ni. Chutia tlang hrang hranga an awm darh zawh tak aṭang chuan nikhua a lo rei chinah chibing hran theuhah an chang zo ta a! Chung ho thlahte kal zel chu tunlaia Mizo hnam zinga Duhlian tawng hmang hnam chi hrang hrang an lo ni ta a ni.</p>
<p>Fei an rawn la leh a, a banglaiah an thiat khat leh ta vek mai a. Chutah Zawlpala chu a inngaihtuah a, a lo tawng ta chu a inchhir em em mai a, tawng hnu leh tui bua a ruh leh theih si lo va, "Ka va tisual tak em! A va pawi thui tak em!" a ti vawng vawng mai a. A lu a na rum rumin a hria a, tih ngaihna dang a awm der tawh hek lo, mittui nen a thlah ta nge nge a. Tualvungi lah tan ngaihna hre lovin a kawlawk reng ta gta mai bawk si a; lunglengin mittui nen an liampui ta hneng hneng a. Zawlpala chuan a lan theih chhûng zawng mittui nen a thlir renga. Nakin lawkah chuan Zawlpala lungleng tuar lo chu Tualvungi te khaw lamah a zin ta a; an inah a va thleng a.</p>
<p>Hmar hnamte phei chuan Lusei thawnthu neih ang hi an nei deuh vek a, thawnthu tawpnaah hian 'Hmanah chuan thlangtla Mizo kan ni a' tiin an tawp ziah bawk. Tin, Mizo hnahthlâk zinga thawnthu hmingthang leh lar ber berte: 'Mangkhaia thawnthu', 'Lalruanga thawnthu', 'Chhura thawnthu', 'Mauruangi thawnthu', 'Rahtea thawnthu', 'Chemtatrawta thawnthu', 'Kungawrhi thawnthu', 'Rimenhawihi thawnthu' leh 'Nungchhaia thawnthu' te hi Burma, India leh Bangladesh-a cheng Mizo hnahthlâk hrang hrangte hian an neih tlan vek a ni.</p>
<p>Tum danga a thinur inhrosain ṭawngkam mawi lo tak taka ka nu a ânkhum hi ka hre fo tawh na a, 'uirenu' tih ṭawngkam chu a hman âwm rêng ka la hre lo. Ka nu nâ ti chu a rúm hawk hawk a, min rawn ban lawm lawm a, mahse, che hman lek lovin ka pa chuan a nghaisa mai si. A chhir, a tum, a pêt. Rui hle lo sela damin an inchhuah lo vang. Ka nu puan bih te chu a phelh nuaih tawh a, insiam thatna hun nei hman hek lo, chhuatah chuan na tuarin a lum kawi nuaih a ni ber e. Kei lah chet ngaihna hre lovin ka lo sual khawih din zum reng ringawt a. Ka pa chuan sawisa tawh lo se ka ti a, ka khap ngam dêr si lo. An thâwm a nat tâk êm aṭang leh ka nu na tuar thâwm chuan zan danga a thâwm a an loh vang nge, kan ṭhenawm hnaite an lo tlan khawm tak tak tih ka hria a.</p>
<p>A hmel ena a fel hmel tehlul nen, dawt sawi hi a ching riau a ni awm e! A pawi khawp mai.</p>
<p>Mikhuala chuan a lo ngaimawh deuh a, "Khai, Pu-a, a tawk e," a han ti zauh mai. Ani lah a lo la duai lo nasa, "Pu-a, te chu mi ti khanglang suh. Nang hlei hlei kha a nia ka huat che! Kan ṭhenawmpa mikhual cham rei satliah mai i ni lo'm ni? Aizawla TKP hruaitu ni ve si, eiruk sim thei si lo, mahni venga eiruk sum hmang ngam bawk si lo, Shillong lo thlen apianga zu rawn in ho hi kan ngaisang lo teh che u a nia," tiin a hau ve ta hrep mai a. Chupa chuan chhan ngaihna vak a hre lo, "Aizawlah TKP a awm love aw!" a ti sup ringawt a.</p>
<p>Saw Sakawr saw a tlân pahin a mawng a vâwr lauh lauh a nih saw.</p>
<p>Chênna hmun hming emaw, hna thawhna hmun hming ang chi emaw kan ziahnaah, hming then hran diat diat kha comma hmanga daidan thin tur a ni.</p>
<p>Pa pakhat hi puan inlukhûpin a rawn kal kun khûn khûn a, naupang hovin an hlau khawp lehnghal a.</p>
<p>Tawng thiamna bulpui 4 intluk tlång veka an pawimawhzia kan sawi tawh a, heng skills palite hi a mal malin an nihna leh pawimawhna te, heng thiamna chi li nei thei tura naupangte kan kaihhruai dan tur tlangpui tal lo chhui leh ila.</p>
<p>Sir, i ti awm ang lo lutuk!</p>
<p>Chawngchen ni khatna "Thingfar zan" pawimawhna dang leh chu, leh Chawngpa tan chauh a ni hek lo. Vawiin thlenga Mizo hnam pum tan a ni. Nula leh tlangval hrai nan Chawngpa chuan a zu tha bik "Sumdeng zu" a han kaichhuak a, an siak eng kulh mai a. Chu chuan nula leh tlangval dangro thawina piah lamah pawimawhna tak a nei a. Tunge in hmasa ber ang? Tuma recommend mamawh lo, lal leh upa te, Val upa te, nula leh tlangvalte leh khawtlangin lungrual taka an hriat tlan, mi kawlh sa kawlh hmaa zam ngai lo, lu chhum ban chhum huama khua leh tui lo chhan fo, tlawmmngai filawrin an in hmasa tur a ni. Tunlai mite ngaiha hun lo takah a biru a, tlangval tho thâng thain an zawng a, an hmuh har phei chuan sumdêng zu in a kham rei thei hle. Mahse tlangval viak thate tuan a tha a, an hmuh veleh an hnuk hawng lui a. Chawngpa chuan mi zawng zawng hmuhah "Huai No" ('No Pui' an ti bawk) chu a hlan ta a. Mipui chuan ropui ti em emin an lo thlir thuap a. Chutiang tluka lawmman sang leh hlu chu thangtharte hian kan nei ve ta lo! English tlangval tana "Knight of Certer" leh, French tlangval tana "Knight of Legion" te, India ram tana "Param vir Chakra" te ai mahin, Mizo tlangval tan zawng a hun lai na na na chuan he "Huai No" inpek hian awmzia a nei lian zawk a, hmaṭang Zonuna khawtlang leh tlangval a vawn that dan hi thangtharte chuan kan suangtuah pha lo hle a, zir tham a tling a ni.</p>
<p>Mizo tawngah hian verb leh adverb inkawp, noun anga ṭang dun hi kan ngah mai a, chûngah chuan verb thu mal kha a indicative mood form a nih chuan chûng verb thu mal indicative mood form leh adverb tang dun chu 'verbal noun' leh 'modifier' inkawp niin, 'noun phrase' a ni thin a, ziah zawm loh tur a ni.</p>
<p>Aih, a lem a nih kha a lem. Mapui in ho mai mai em mai.</p>

<p>Zawlbûk-a tuah ên tûr leh a lum ai tûrin thing a duh tam khawp mai a. Tlangvalin an duh tâwka an han vûr ngat phei chu a alhin khanchhuk a hliau pêl zuai zuai thei a. <p>Eng pawh nise, hlim i duh tak tak chuan nui ve phawt teh le! <p>Tunah chuan mi tam takin sum khawl khawm nachang an hre ta.</p>
<p>Mizo history ziaktu hrang hrangten Mizo tobul nia an hriat leh an chhui dan aṭanga kan thlir dan kan tarlang ta a. Tunah chuan kan theih ang tawka kan dapa kan chhui ve dan kan vawrhchhuak ve thung dawn a ni. Tun hmaa kan lo ziak thin nen tuna kan sawi hi inan lohna lai a awm zeuh zeuh thei a. Hei hi kan chhuizawm zelnaa kan hriat belh zel aṭanga kan hmuh dan a ni a. Tlema kimchang zawk deuh a nih kan ring a, tun hmaa kan ziak ai chuan a chian deuh hlek zawk pawh kan beisei.</p>
<p>Han pak zaih zaih rawh le.</p>
<p>Tih tak takah chuan thawnthu phuah tawh leh ka phuah mêk pawh hi Zotei vang ka ti lo thei lo. Zotei hi ka tan chuan 'Muse' a ni ber e. Hmanlai chuan Greek-hote ngaih dan chuan an rimawi pathian khan hla a phuahtir niin an ngai a, kei erawh chu thawnthu min phuahtir hlauh a nih hi. Ani nen hian intawng hlauh lo ila chu heti ang khawvelah hian ka chêng lo vang a, heti ang thawnthu hi ka phuah kher lo vang.</p>
<p>Tin, 14th May, 2021 khan Wuhan-ah thlipui leh ruahsur nasa takin Wuhan khawpui a nuai a. Tin, China hmun hrang hrang Yunnan leh Southern China-ah Lirnghing na tak Deadly Earthquake an tih mai chuan hmun hrang hrang a sawi a, Southern Qinghai-ah te chuan 7.4 magnitude-a nain a nghing bawk a, mi tam takin hliam an tuar a, thihpui pawh an awm nual mai. Hmun hrang hranga Lirnghing leh thlipui tleh leh ruahsur nasa leh tek tla te, thawngaleivir kan tih mai te, a thenah kangmei chhuak leh khawkheng te leh chhiatna chi hrang hrangin khawvel a tuam hlup hlup mai hi a makin a rapthlâk a ni. Kum 2021-a khawvel hmun hrang hranga chhiatna thleng hi a makin a rapthlâk khawp mai. Heihi a niang hri leh chhiatna thleng tur kan Bible-in min lo hrilh vek tawh kha. Chanchin Tha Luka Ziak Bung 21:10-11-ah chuan ti hian a lo inziak a, "Hnam hrang leh hnam hrang an indo vang a, ram hrang leh ram hrang an indo vang a; lir nasa takin a nghing a nghing ang a; hmun hrang hrangah tamte a tlaṭang a, hrite a leng bawk ang a; van aṭangin thil hlauhawmte leh chhinchhiahna nasa takte a lo awm ang," tiin. Tunah hian kan Bible-in a lo sawi ang hian he hun khirh tak leh rapthlâk tak hi kan tawng mek a ni. Manganna leh chungpikna pawh a la zual zel dawn a nih hmel.</p>
<p>Pi duhtak, lo ngawi rih la, ka'n chhiar chhunzawm ang e. Leilung mawitu, ka thusawi chu ringhlel suh ang che. Mangtha. Mihring ka nih chhûnga i tana rinawm tur.</p>

<p>An party-ah a tla tlum hle.</p>
<p>Thumal pakhat âia tam ziah zawma solid compound word kan chher zingah, mood inthlâk aṭanga a ziah dan kan tih danglam thin an awm leh a. Chúng solid compound word kan tih danglam dan chuan kalphung (inflection rule) fel tak a nei a. Thumal hawrawp lâita chauh thlâk danglam thin te, thumal hawrawp tâwp chauh thlâk danglam thin te, thumal hawrawp lâita leh a tâwp hawrawp thlâk danglam thin te a awm a ni.</p>
<p>Nia, kil tin aṭangin i veng vek tih ka lo hre lo a ni, ka rilru a dam ta huai e. Keimah zawk hi ka inthiam lo zawk daih a nia, a chhan chu i buai lohna turah ka hnuk lut che a, i tawrh phah ta hrep bawk si a. Inthiam lohna tur pakhat mah i nei hlei nem, hei hi ka buaina dik tak a ni.</p>
